## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[Start Test Suite] --> B[test_validate_put]
    A --> C[test_validate_put_with_not_null_id]
    A --> D[test_validate_put_with_missing_fields]
    B --> B1[Create TripLeg]
    B1 --> B2[Set all required fields]
    B2 --> B3[Call validator.validate]
    B3 --> B4[No exception - PASS]
    C --> C1[Create TripLeg with ID]
    C1 --> C2[Set all required fields]
    C2 --> C3[Call validator.validate]
    C3 --> C4[No exception - PASS]
    D --> D1[Create empty TripLeg]
    D1 --> D2[Validate - expect ValidationError]
    D2 --> D3{All fields missing?}
    D3 -->|Yes| D4[Add solution_id]
    D4 --> D5[Validate - expect ValidationError]
    D5 --> D6[Add owner_organization_fv_id]
    D6 --> D7[Validate - expect ValidationError]
    D7 --> D8[Add carrier_organization_fv_id]
    D8 --> D9[Validate - expect ValidationError]
    D9 --> D10[Add destination_location_code]
    D10 --> D11[Validate - expect ValidationError]
    D11 --> D12[Add origin_location_code]
    D12 --> D13[Validate - expect ValidationError]
    D13 --> D14[Add creator_shipment_id]
    D14 --> D15[Validate - expect ValidationError]
    D15 --> D16[Add sequence_number]
    D16 --> D17[Validate - expect invalid type error]
    D17 --> D18[Set type to PLANNED]
    D18 --> D19[Set shipment_number]
    D19 --> D20[Validate - PASS]
    D20 --> E[End Test Suite]
    B4 --> E
    C4 --> E
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Test as PutTripLegValidatorTest
    participant TripLeg as TripLeg
    participant Validator as TripLegValidator
    participant Error as ValidationError
    Test->>TripLeg: Create TripLeg()
    TripLeg-->>Test: trip_leg instance
    Test->>TripLeg: Set required fields
    Test->>Validator: validate(trip_leg, "PUT")
    Validator->>TripLeg: Check solution_id
    Validator->>TripLeg: Check owner_organization_fv_id
    Validator->>TripLeg: Check carrier_organization_fv_id
    Validator->>TripLeg: Check destination_location_code
    Validator->>TripLeg: Check origin_location_code
    Validator->>TripLeg: Check shipment_number or creator_shipment_id
    Validator->>TripLeg: Check sequence_number
    Validator->>TripLeg: Check type
    alt Valid TripLeg
        Validator-->>Test: Success
    else Missing fields
        Validator->>Error: Create ValidationError
        Error-->>Test: Raise exception
    else Invalid type
        Validator->>Error: Create ValidationError
        Error-->>Test: Raise exception
    end
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> EmptyTripLeg
    EmptyTripLeg --> SolutionIdSet: Set solution_id
    SolutionIdSet --> OwnerOrgSet: Set owner_organization_fv_id
    OwnerOrgSet --> CarrierOrgSet: Set carrier_organization_fv_id
    CarrierOrgSet --> DestinationSet: Set destination_location_code
    DestinationSet --> OriginSet: Set origin_location_code
    OriginSet --> ShipmentIdSet: Set creator_shipment_id or shipment_number
    ShipmentIdSet --> SequenceSet: Set sequence_number
    SequenceSet --> TypeSet: Set type (PLANNED or ACTUAL)
    TypeSet --> ValidTripLeg: Validation passes
    ValidTripLeg --> [*]
    EmptyTripLeg --> ValidationError: validate() without fields
    SolutionIdSet --> ValidationError: validate() missing fields
    OwnerOrgSet --> ValidationError: validate() missing fields
    CarrierOrgSet --> ValidationError: validate() missing fields
    DestinationSet --> ValidationError: validate() missing fields
    OriginSet --> ValidationError: validate() missing fields
    ShipmentIdSet --> ValidationError: validate() missing fields
    SequenceSet --> ValidationError: validate() missing type
    ValidationError --> [*]
```
